# <a name="obsolete-members-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="c8e3a-102">Membri obsoleti in .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c8e3a-102">Obsolete Members in the .NET Framework</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c8e3a-103">Nelle tabelle di questo articolo sono elencati i tipi obsoleti in .NET Framework 4.5 e versioni successive, organizzati per assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c8e3a-103">The tables in this article list the type members that are obsolete in the .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c8e3a-104">Usare i seguenti collegamenti per vedere un elenco di membri obsoleti e le alternative consigliate in ogni assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c8e3a-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete members and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c8e3a-105">In questo articolo non sono elencati i membri dei tipi obsoleti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c8e3a-105">This article doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c8e3a-106">Per un elenco dei tipi obsoleti, vedere [Tipi obsoleti](obsolete-types.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c8e3a-106">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete Types](obsolete-types.md).</span></span>

<a name="SystemMembers"></a>   
## <a name="obsolete-members-in-system-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="c8e3a-140">Membri obsoleti negli assembly di sistema</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c8e3a-140">Obsolete Members in System Assemblies</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="c8e3a-141">Nelle tabelle seguenti sono elencati i membri obsoleti negli assembly di sistema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c8e3a-141">The following tables list the obsolete members in system assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c8e3a-142">Questi assembly vengono usati per lo sviluppo di applicazioni generiche destinate a .NET Framework.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c8e3a-142">These assemblies are used for general\-purpose application development that targets the .NET Framework.</span></span>
